IBM is making significant advancements in cloud-native AI supercomputing in Switzerland, focusing on both hardware and software infrastructure. Here's a breakdown of their efforts:

**Key Advancements and Initiatives:**

*   **Collaboration with Phoenix Technologies:** IBM has partnered with Phoenix Technologies in Switzerland to deliver an end-to-end, on-premises cloud-native AI supercomputer. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) The first phase of this system came online in mid-August 2024. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) This collaboration aims to create a local AI hub for Phoenix's customers, providing sovereign AI applications through their kvant AI cloud solution. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **AI Innovation Center:** IBM Research and Phoenix Technologies are collaborating to establish an AI Innovation Center in Switzerland. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **AIU-Spyre Deployment:** In 2025, IBM plans to expand its AI supercomputing capabilities in Switzerland with a scale-out deployment of AIU-Spyre, an AI accelerator designed by IBM Research. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Zurich Research Laboratory:** IBM has maintained a research laboratory in Switzerland since 1956. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [embed2scale](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) The Zurich lab focuses on developing next-generation data and AI technologies to address business and societal challenges, including accelerating the discovery of new materials, understanding climate impact, scaling AI in business workflows, and optimizing the cost/performance of data-intensive applications. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2)
*   **ETH-IBM Discovery Accelerator Hub Program:** IBM and the AI Center of ETH Zurich have a four-year collaboration (started in January 2024) to advance AI for scientific discovery applications. [ethz](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) The program focuses on multi-modal foundation models for science and trustworthy AI for discovery. [ethz](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4)
*   **IBM and CoreWeave Partnership:** CoreWeave is partnering with IBM to deliver a next-generation AI supercomputer, utilizing NVIDIA's GB200 Grace Blackwell systems on a supercomputing scale. [techerati](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) IBM plans to use CoreWeave's platform to train and develop future generations of its Granite models. [techerati](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6)

**Hardware Infrastructure:**

*   **NVIDIA H100 GPUs:** The cloud-native AI supercomputer solution can scale from dozens to hundreds or thousands of NVIDIA H100 GPUs. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **RDMA-enabled Ethernet Network:** The solution includes a flexible, scalable, and affordable RDMA-enabled Ethernet-based network to support high-performance AI training. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **IBM Storage Scale:** A high-performance storage system based on IBM Storage Scale, is used. [techerati](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [futurumgroup](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) IBM Storage Scale is also known as GPFS, has been well-known and used in the HPC clusters. [futurumgroup](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
*   **Intel Gaudi 3 AI Accelerators:** IBM Cloud is the first cloud service provider to deploy Intel Gaudi 3 AI accelerators. [intel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) Customers can use Gaudi 3 via IBM Cloud Virtual Servers on the IBM Virtual Private Cloud (VPC). [intel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8)
*   **NVIDIA GB200 Grace Blackwell Systems:** The supercomputer being developed in partnership with CoreWeave will be one of the first to utilize NVIDIA's GB200 Grace Blackwell systems on a supercomputing scale. [techerati](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6)
*   **NVIDIA Quantum-2 InfiniBand:** Interconnect will be provided using NVIDIA Quantum-2 InfiniBand networking, ensuring high-speed communication between systems. [techerati](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5)
*   **NVMe Flash Technology:** The supercomputer will leverage IBM Storage Scale System, combined with NVMe flash technology, to provide high-performance storage for demanding AI workloads. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [techerati](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5)

**Software Infrastructure:**

*   **OpenShift Container Platform and OpenShift AI:** The solution contains a cloud-native AI platform based on OpenShift Container Platform and OpenShift AI. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **watsonx.ai:** Access to watsonx.ai is provided as needed. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Pre-built Containers and AI Models:** The software stack offers pre-built containers, AI models, and tools for generative AI innovation. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Automation and APIs:** The AI infrastructure can be provisioned and accessed elastically through APIs, similar to a public cloud. [ibm](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **IBM Cloud Virtual Servers:** Customers can use Gaudi 3 via IBM Cloud Virtual Servers on the IBM Virtual Private Cloud (VPC). [intel](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8)
*   **Red Hat OpenShift and watsonx AI Platform Support:** Support for Red Hat OpenShift and IBM's watsonx AI platform is expected to be available this quarter (Q2/Q3 2025).
*   **IBM Storage Scale with Content Aware Storage (CAS):** IBM announced content-aware Storage Scale for AI Workloads, addressing requirements for faster response to data changes and data silos with the AI data pipeline. [futurumgroup](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)

These advancements demonstrate IBM's commitment to advancing cloud-native AI supercomputing in Switzerland, with a focus on providing scalable, high-performance infrastructure and software solutions for AI research, development, and deployment.

Based on the search results, here's a synthesis of the criteria used to determine top tech companies in Zurich, considering factors like revenue, employee count, innovation, and market share:

**General Ranking Methodologies:**

*   **Measurable Success Factors and Employee Experience:** Top tech companies in Switzerland are ranked based on measurable success factors and real employee experiences, including innovation capabilities, work environment quality, and employee well-being. [nucamp](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) \[2]
*   **Algorithm-Based Scoring:** Some rankings use an algorithm that scores startups based on total investment, employee count, and quarterly website traffic. [startupblink](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) \[5] [deeptechnation](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [nucamp](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3) [swisslinx](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) [nucamp](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)
*   **Employee Satisfaction:** Employee feedback and in-depth analysis of HR processes are also considered for company rankings. \[12, 13] [greatplacetowork](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)
*   **Seedtable Score:** A dynamic score using quantitative and qualitative data points to signal the momentum behind a company. [seedtable](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) \[4]

**Specific Criteria and Factors:**
